colleges\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        8 technical colleges\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        24 independent non-profit colleges\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Libraries">\n        Libraries\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Ohio is home to some of the nation\'s highest-ranked public libraries.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-haplr_147-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-haplr-147">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hennen%27s_American_Public_Library_Ratings" title="Hennen\'s American Public Library Ratings">\n        2008 study by Thomas J. Hennen Jr.\n       </a>\n       ranked Ohio as number one in a state-by-state comparison.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">\n        <a href="#cite_note-148">\n         [148]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       For 2008, 31 of Ohio\'s library systems were all ranked in the top ten for American cities of their population category.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-haplr_147-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-haplr-147">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        500,000 books or more\n        <ul>\n         <li>\n          <a href="/wiki/Columbus_Metropolitan_Library" title="Columbus Metropolitan Library">\n           Columbus Metropolitan Library\n          </a>\n          (First)\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <a href="/wiki/Cuyahoga_County_Public_Library" title="Cuyahoga County Public Library">\n           Cuyahoga County Public Library\n          </a>\n          (Second)\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <a href="/wiki/Public_Library_of_Cincinnati_and_Hamilton_County" title="Public Library of Cincinnati and Hamilton County">\n           Public Library of Cincinnati and Hamilton County\n          </a>\n          (Tenth)\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ohio_Public_Library_Information_Network_(OPLIN)" title="Ohio Public Library Information Network (OPLIN)">\n        Ohio Public Library Information Network (OPLIN)\n       </a>\n       is an organization that provides Ohio residents with internet access to their 251 public libraries. OPLIN also provides Ohioans with free home access to high-quality, subscription research databases.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ohio also offers the\n       <a href="/wiki/OhioLINK" title="OhioLINK">\n        OhioLINK\n       </a>\n       program, allowing Ohio\'s libraries (particularly those from colleges and universities) access to materials for the other libraries. The program is largely successful in allowing researchers for access to books and other media that might not be otherwise available.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">\n        Culture\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Arts">\n        Arts\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">\n          <img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text">\n         <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          <b>\n           This section needs expansion\n          </b>\n          .\n          <small>\n           You can help by\n           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Ohio&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">\n            adding to it\n           </a>\n           .\n          </small>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (September 2017)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">\n        Sports\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sport_in_Ohio" title="Sport in Ohio">\n        Sport in Ohio\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Professional_sports_teams">\n        Professional sports teams\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Ohio is home to major professional sports teams in baseball, basketball,\n       <a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">\n        football\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ice_hockey" title="Ice hockey">\n        hockey\n       </a>\n       , lacrosse and soccer. The state\'s major professional sporting teams include:\n       <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Reds" title="Cincinnati Reds">\n        Cincinnati Reds\n       </a>\n       (Major League Baseball),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">\n        <a href="#cite_note-149">\n         [149]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Ohio_Machine" title="Ohio Machine">\n        Ohio Machine\n       </a>\n       (Major League Lacrosse),\n       <a href="/wiki/Cleveland_Indians" title="Cleveland Indians">\n        Cleveland Indians\n       </a>\n       (Major League Baseball),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">\n        <a href="#cite_note-150">\n         [150]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Bengals" title="Cincinnati Bengals">\n        Cincinnati Bengals\n       </a>\n       (National Football League),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NFL_151-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NFL-151">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Cleveland_Browns" title="Cleveland Browns">\n        Cleveland Browns\n       </a>\n       (National Football League),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NFL_151-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NFL-151">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Cleveland_Cavaliers" title="Cleveland Cavaliers">\n        Cleveland Cavaliers\n       </a>\n       (National Basketball Association),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">\n        <a href="#cite_note-152">\n         [152]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Columbus_Blue_Jackets" title="Columbus Blue Jackets">\n        Columbus Blue Jackets\n       </a>\n       (National Hockey League),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153">\n        <a href="#cite_note-153">\n         [153]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Columbus_Crew" title="Columbus Crew">\n        Columbus Crew\n       </a>\n       (Major League Soccer).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154">\n        <a href="#cite_note-154">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ohio played a central role in the development of both Major League Baseball and the National Football League. Baseball\'s first fully professional team, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Red_Stockings" title="Cincinnati Red Stockings">\n        Cincinnati Red Stockings\n       </a>\n       of 1869, were organized in Ohio.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155">\n        <a href="#cite_note-155">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An informal early 20th century American football association, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ohio_League" title="Ohio League">\n        Ohio League\n       </a>\n       , was the direct predecessor of the NFL, although neither of Ohio\'s modern NFL franchises trace their roots to an Ohio League club. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Pro_Football_Hall_of_Fame" title="Pro Football Hall of Fame">\n        Pro Football Hall of Fame\n       </a>\n       is located in\n       <a href="/wiki/Canton,_Ohio" title="Canton, Ohio">\n        Canton\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On a smaller scale, Ohio hosts\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Minor_league_baseball" title="Minor league baseball">\n        minor league baseball\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Arena_football" title="Arena football">\n        arena football\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Indoor_American_football" title="Indoor American football">\n        indoor football\n       </a>\n       , mid-level hockey, and lower division soccer.\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Individual_sports">\n        Individual sports\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Mid-Ohio_Sports_Car_Course" title="Mid-Ohio Sports Car Course">\n        Mid-Ohio Sports Car Course\n       </a>\n       has hosted several auto racing championships, including\n       <a href="/wiki/CART_World_Series" title="CART World Series">\n        CART World Series\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/IndyCar_Series" title="IndyCar Series">\n        IndyCar Series\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/NASCAR" title="NASCAR">\n        NASCAR\n       </a>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nationwide_Series" title="Nationwide Series">\n        Nationwide Series\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Can-Am" title="Can-Am">\n        Can-Am\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Formula_5000" title="Formula 5000">\n        Formula 5000\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/IMSA_GT_Championship" title="IMSA GT Championship">\n        IMSA GT Championship\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Le_Mans_Series" title="American Le Mans Series">\n        American Le Mans Series\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Rolex_Sports_Car_Series" title="Rolex Sports Car Series">\n        Rolex Sports Car Series\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Prix_of_Cleveland" title="Grand Prix of Cleveland">\n        Grand Prix of Cleveland\n       </a>\n       also hosted CART races from 1982 to 2007. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Eldora_Speedway" title="Eldora Speedway">\n        Eldora Speedway\n       </a>\n       is a major dirt oval that hosts NASCAR\n       <a href="/wiki/Camping_World_Truck_Series" title="Camping World Truck Series">\n        Camping World Truck Series\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/World_of_Outlaws" title="World of Outlaws">\n        World of Outlaws\n       </a>\n       Sprint Cars and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USAC_Silver_Crown_Series" title="USAC Silver Crown Series">\n        USAC Silver Crown Series\n       </a>\n       races.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ohio hosts two\n       <a href="/wiki/PGA_Tour" title="PGA Tour">\n        PGA Tour\n       </a>\n       events, the\n       <a href="/wiki/WGC-Bridgestone_Invitational" title="WGC-Bridgestone Invitational">\n        WGC-Bridgestone Invitational\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Memorial_Tournament" title="Memorial Tournament">\n        Memorial Tournament\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Masters" title="Cincinnati Masters">\n        Cincinnati Masters\n       </a>\n       is an\n       <a href="/wiki/ATP_World_Tour_Masters_1000" title="ATP World Tour Masters 1000">\n        ATP World Tour Masters 1000\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/WTA_Premier_tournaments" title="WTA Premier tournaments">\n        WTA Premier 5\n       </a>\n       tennis tournament.\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="College_sports">\n        College sports\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Ohio has eight\n       <a href="/wiki/NCAA_Division_I_Football_Bowl_Subdivision" title="NCAA Division I Football Bowl Subdivision">\n        NCAA Division I FBS\n       </a>\n       college football teams, divided among three different\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_NCAA_conferences" title="List of NCAA conferences">\n        conferences\n       </a>\n       . It has also experienced considerable success in the secondary and tertiary tiers of college football divisions.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In Division I-A, representing the\n       <a href="/wiki/Big_Ten_Conference" title="Big Ten Conference">\n        Big Ten\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ohio_State_Buckeyes_football" title="Ohio State Buckeyes football">\n        Ohio State Buckeyes football\n       </a>\n       team ranks 5th among all-time winningest programs,\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2014)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       with seven national championships and seven\n       <a href="/wiki/Heisman_Trophy" title="Heisman Trophy">\n        Heisman Trophy\n       </a>\n       winners. Their biggest rivals are the Michigan Wolverines, whom they traditionally play each year as the last game of their regular season schedule.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Ohio has six teams represented in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mid-American_Conference" title="Mid-American Conference">\n        Mid-American Conference\n       </a>\n       : the\n       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Akron" title="University of Akron">\n        University of Akron\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bowling_Green_State_University" title="Bowling Green State University">\n        Bowling Green\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Kent_State_University" title="Kent State University">\n        Kent State\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Miami_University" title="Miami University">\n        Miami University\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ohio_University" title="Ohio University">\n        Ohio University\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Toledo" title="University of Toledo">\n        University of Toledo\n       </a>\n       . The MAC headquarters are in Cleveland. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Bearcats_football" title="Cincinnati Bearcats football">\n        University of Cincinnati Bearcats\n       </a>\n       represent Ohio in the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Athletic_Conference" title="American Athletic Conference">\n        American Athletic Conference\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="State_symbols">\n        State symbols\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_Ohio_state_symbols" title="List of Ohio state symbols">\n        List of Ohio state symbols\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lists_of_U.S._state_insignia" title="Lists of U.S. state insignia">\n        Lists of U.S. state insignia\n       </a>\n symbols:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        State capital:\n        <a href="/wiki/Columbus,_Ohio" title="Columbus, Ohio">\n         Columbus\n        </a>\n        <sup class="reference"
